- 来源：VOA Learning English - Education Tips
- 发布时间：2025-02-18T22:25:00+00:00
- 优先级分数：15
- 推荐级别：观察中

- 摘要：Some studies have shown that for learners to fully understand a written work, they need to know 95 percent or more of the words in it. That means that if there are only five or more words you do not know in a 100-word text, you might not really understand it!
- 中文速读：相关动态提供了科技、研究或教育领域的新背景，可先记录关键信号，等待更明确的公共议题出现。

- 发布时间：2025-01-14T22:05:00+00:00

- 重复原因：无
- 首次推送日期：无
- 标签：AI, 教育研究
- 链接：https://learningenglish.voanews.com/a/students-with-disabilities-praise-assistive-technology-using-ai/7926297.html
- 摘要：Artificial intelligence (AI) is being used to help students with visual, speech, language and hearing disabilities. Schools in the United States are developing methods for how to use AI and are trying out new applications.
- 中文速读：内容聚焦教育、学习或高校场景，适合关注技术变化如何影响学生、教师和家庭的日常选择。
- 选题判断：适合七点半爸爸主稿，可写成 AI、学校学习或数字生活如何进入普通家庭决策的角度，重点放在家长能理解的变化。
- 七爸选题建议：适合写成主稿，角度可定为“AI 家教真的能帮孩子学数学吗”。重点解释工具如何提升练习反馈、信心和学习效率，同时提醒家长别把陪伴、诊断和鼓励完全交给系统。 可作为早间选题会的辅助判断。

- 摘要：This week, we give you more information about a common sentence pattern in English: the linking verb pattern. Learning how to use linking verb patterns will help you improve your writing. You can think about creative ways to use them, or you can learn to recognize when you use them too often.
